\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Class to manage Clothoid Curve. A clothoid curve is described by the following generalized Fresnel integrals

\[
  \begin{cases}
     x(s) = x_0 + \displaystyle\int_0^s \cos(as^2+bs+c) \mathrm{d}t \\[1em]
     y(s) = y_0 + \displaystyle\int_0^s \sin(as^2+bs+c) \mathrm{d}t
  \end{cases}
\]

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ClothoidCurve()}{ClothoidCurve()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/7]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_g2lib_1_1_clothoid_curve_a5e7c49faeb843a647a8a075660cab81d} 
G2lib\+::\+Clothoid\+Curve\+::\+Clothoid\+Curve (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}} const}]{P0}{\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}}}]{theta0}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}} const}]{P1}{\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}}}]{theta1}{, }\item[{string const \&}]{name}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [explicit]}}

Construct a clothoid $ \G(s) $ solving the G1 problem.

\[
  \begin{cases}
    G(0) = \mathbf{p}_0 & \\[1em]
    G(L) = \mathbf{p}_1 & \\[1em]
    G\textnormal{\textquotesingle}(0) = (\cos\theta_0,\sin\theta_0)^T & \\[1em]
    G\textnormal{\textquotesingle}(L) = (\cos\theta_1,\sin\theta_1)^T & \\[1em]
  \end{cases}
\]


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em P0} & initial point $ \mathbf{p}_0 $ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em theta0} & initial angle $ \theta_0 $ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em P1} & final point $ \mathbf{p}_1 $ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em theta1} & final angle $ \theta_1 $ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em name} & name of the clothoid curve \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_g2lib_1_1_clothoid_curve_a81829b959c99694ff61e4daad18e4853} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_a17146eb1606475bedc9a2d27f3b29e34}{integer}} G2lib\+::\+Clothoid\+Curve\+::closest\+\_\+point\+\_\+\+ISO (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}}}]{qx}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}}}]{qy}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}} \&}]{x}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}} \&}]{y}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}} \&}]{s}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}} \&}]{t}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}} \&}]{dst}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Compute the point on clothoid at minimal distance from a given point using the optimized algorithm described in the publication\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{E.\+Bertolazzi, M.\+Frego}}, Point-\/\+Clothoid distance and projection computation SIAM J. Scientific Computing, Vol. 41, No. 5, pp. A3326-\/\+A3353
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em qx} & x-\/coordinate of the given point \\
\hline
{\em qy} & y-\/coordinate of the given point \\
\hline
{\em x} & x-\/coordinate of the point on clothoid at minimal distance \\
\hline
{\em y} & y-\/coordinate of the point on clothoid at minimal distance \\
\hline
{\em s} & curvilinear coordinate of the point (X,Y) on the clothoid \\
\hline
{\em t} & normal coordinate of the point (X,Y) on the clothoid \\
\hline
{\em dst} & the distance of the point from the clothoid \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 = point is projected orthogonal 0 = more than one projection (first returned) -\/1 = minimum point is not othogonal projection to curve 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g2lib_1_1_base_curve_abfa1b5a7ebf24a6068512df027025a4f}{G2lib\+::\+Base\+Curve}}.
